) AS [t0] ON [b].[BookingId] = [t0].[BookingsBookingId]

    SELECT [b1].[BookingsBookingId], [b1].[DoctorsId], [d].[Id], [d].[AccessFailedCount], [d].[ConcurrencyStamp], [d].[Email], [d].[EmailConfirmed], [d].[Fees], [d].[Hospital], [d].[LockoutEnabled], [d].[LockoutEnd], [d].[Name], [d].[NormalizedEmail], [d].[NormalizedUserName], [d].[PasswordHash], [d].[PhoneNumber], [d].[PhoneNumberConfirmed], [d].[Qualifications], [d].[SecurityStamp], [d].[Specialization], [d].[TwoFactorEnabled], [d].[UserName]

    INNER JOIN [Doctors] AS [d] ON [b1].[DoctorsId] = [d].[Id]
) AS [t1] ON [t].[BookingId] = [t1].[BookingsBookingId]
